   "source": [
    "# A small function for looking into the unique values\n",
    "# usually we can write like df['column'].unique or np.unique(df['column'])\n",
    "\n",
    "def print_unique(df):\n",
    "    for col in df:\n",
    "        print(\"unique values for column : \",col,\":number of unique values:\",len(df[col].unique()))\n",
    "        print(df[col].unique())\n",
    "        print(\"#\"*150)\n",
    "\n",
    "print_unique(df)"
   ]

   "source": [
    "# A small function for looking into the unique values\n",
    "# usually we can write like df['column'].unique or np.unique(df['column'])\n",
    "\n",
    "def print_unique(df):\n",
    "    for col in df:\n",
    "        print(\"unique values for column : \",col,\":number of unique values:\",len(df[col].unique()))\n",
    "        print(df[col].value_counts())\n",
    "        print(\"#\"*150)\n",
    "\n",
    "print_unique(df)"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "# columns with more than 80% nulls,these are the columns which we can drop directly\n",
    "filter=((df.isnull().sum()/df.shape[0])*100)>80\n",
    "df_to_delete=df.loc[: ,filter.values].columns\n",
    "delete_columns=list(df_to_delete)\n",
    "delete_columns\n",
    "#Identify variables with null values\n",
    "filter_=((df.isnull().sum()/df.shape[0])*100)>0\n",
    "df_with_nulls=df.loc[: ,filter_.values].columns\n",
    "null_columns=list(df_with_nulls)\n",
    "null_columns"
   ]
